	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Sergio Busquets</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>

		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Spanish association football player</div>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">In this <a href="/wiki/Spanish_name" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish name">Spanish name</a>, the first or paternal&#32;<a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">surname</a> is <i> Busquets</i>&#32;and the second or maternal family name is <i> Burgos</i>.</div>

<p><b>Sergio Busquets Burgos</b> (<small>Catalan:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Catalan" title="Help:IPA/Catalan">[buskts]</a></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <small>Spanish:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">[sexjo uskets]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;A&#93;</a></sup> born 16 July 1988) is a Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain national team</a>. He is considered to be a deep lying playmaker capable of directing the game play through short and calm passes.<sup id="cite_ref-busquets_ranked_1_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-busquets_ranked_1-5">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-busquets_ranked_2_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-busquets_ranked_2-6">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-busquets_ranked_3_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-busquets_ranked_3-7">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-busquets_ranked_4_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-busquets_ranked_4-8">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/List_of_one-club_men_in_association_football" title="List of one-club men in association football">one-club man</a>, he arrived in Barcelona's first team in July 2008, and made over 600 total appearances. He was part of their squads that won a <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a> of <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a>, <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_FC_Barcelona_season" title="200809 FC Barcelona season">200809</a> and <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_FC_Barcelona_season" title="201415 FC Barcelona season">201415</a>.
</p><p>Busquets made his senior international debut for Spain in April 2009. He helped the country win the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">Euro 2012</a> tournaments, and also featured at two other <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cups</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Sabadell" title="Sabadell">Sabadell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Province_of_Barcelona" title="Province of Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a>, Busquets began playing football with local team CD Badia del Vallès,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> followed by spells with CEF Barberà Andalucía, <a href="/wiki/UE_Lleida" title="UE Lleida">UE Lleida</a> and UFB Jàbac Terrassa,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> before joining <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>'s youth ranks in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-BLAU_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BLAU-11">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He scored seven goals in 26 games for the <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona_(youth)" title="FC Barcelona (youth)"><i>Juvenil A</i> team</a> in his second season and, two years later, Busquets was promoted to the <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona_B" title="FC Barcelona B">B team</a> under <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a>, and helped them <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Tercera_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="200708 Tercera División">achieve promotion</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n_B" title="Segunda División B">third division</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In that same season he would make his first-team debut, coming on as a <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Copa_Catalunya" title="Copa Catalunya">Copa Catalunya</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:25%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Positionally, he seems like a veteran with or without the ball. With the ball he makes what is difficult look easy: he disposes of the ball with one or two touches. Without the ball, he gives us a lesson: that of being in the right place to intercept and running just to recover the ball."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Johan Cruyff, 15 September 2008<sup id="cite_ref-Periódico_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Periódico-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 13 September 2008, Busquets played his first <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> match, featuring 90 minutes in a 11 home draw to <a href="/wiki/Racing_de_Santander" title="Racing de Santander">Racing de Santander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> During Barcelona's <a href="/wiki/2008-09_UEFA_Champions_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2008-09 UEFA Champions League">2008-09 UEFA Champions League</a> clash against <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a> at <a href="/wiki/St._Jakob-Park" title="St. Jakob-Park">St. Jakob-Park</a> on 22 October 2008, he scored the second goal in the 15th minute in a 50 <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_C" title="200809 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> win;<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> in early December, in another start, he scored his second with <i>Barça</i> in the competition, netting in the 83rd minute of a 23 home loss against <a href="/wiki/FC_Shakhtar_Donetsk" title="FC Shakhtar Donetsk">Shakhtar Donetsk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:S._Busquets_(2009-05).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg/220px-S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg/330px-S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg/440px-S._Busquets_%282009-05%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="533" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:S._Busquets_(2009-05).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Busquets attending a press conference for <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in 2009</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 December 2008, Busquets signed a contract extension until 2013 with a buy-out clause of 80&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> On 7 March 2009 he scored his first league goal, in a 20 home win over <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 27 May 2009, having been regularly played as he competed for the spot with internationals <a href="/wiki/Seydou_Keita_(footballer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Seydou Keita (footballer)">Seydou Keita</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yaya_Tour%C3%A9" title="Yaya Touré">Yaya Touré</a>, he also featured in Barcelona's starting eleven in the <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2009 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League final</a>, a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rome" title="Rome">Rome</a>; with that victory, <a href="/wiki/Carles_Busquets" title="Carles Busquets">Carles Busquets</a> and Sergio Busquets became only the third father-and-son combo to both have won Europe's top club competition playing for the same team, joining <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Sanch%C3%ADs_Mart%C3%ADnez" class="mw-redirect" title="Manuel Sanchís Martínez">Manuel Sanchís Martínez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Sanch%C3%ADs_Hontiyuelo" class="mw-redirect" title="Manuel Sanchís Hontiyuelo">Manuel Sanchís Hontiyuelo</a> (won it with <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Cesare_Maldini" title="Cesare Maldini">Cesare Maldini</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a> (<a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Busquets' fine form continued in the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_FC_Barcelona_season" title="200910 FC Barcelona season">200910 campaign</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> with Guardiola preferring him to Touré as Barcelona's central holding midfielder. In the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Semi-finals" title="200910 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League semi-final</a> 10 victory (and an eventual 23 aggregate defeat) against <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> at <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> on 28 April 2010, he went down to the ground after <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Motta" title="Thiago Motta">Thiago Motta</a> had raised his arm and appeared to push Busquets directly in the face.<sup id="cite_ref-DT_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DT-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> As a result of this action, the former was shown a <a href="/wiki/Red_card_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Red card (association football)">red card</a> and dismissed for violent conduct, whilst the latter was subsequently criticised by both Motta and the media for apparently feigning injury.<sup id="cite_ref-DT_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DT-25">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Busquets was again ever-present in <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_FC_Barcelona_season" title="201011 FC Barcelona season">201011</a>, even playing as a <a href="/wiki/Central_defender" class="mw-redirect" title="Central defender">centre back</a> on occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 27 January 2011, he signed a contract extension that would keep him at the club until 2015&#160; the buyout clause was increased to 150&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On 8 March 2011, playing at centre back, he scored an <a href="/wiki/Own_goal" title="Own goal">own goal</a> from a <a href="/wiki/Corner_kick" title="Corner kick">corner kick</a> against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, in <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Round_of_16" title="201011 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">the season's Champions League round-of-16</a>, levelling the score at 11; Barcelona eventually won the game 31 (and 43 on aggregate).<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> On 28 May, Busquets played the full match during his side's 31 <a href="/wiki/2011_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2011 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions league final</a> victory against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 24 April 2012, Busquets scored a rare goal  only his sixth official one in four years  netting from an easy tap-in after an <a href="/wiki/Isaac_Cuenca" title="Isaac Cuenca">Isaac Cuenca</a> cross to make it 10 for the hosts in the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Semi-finals" title="201112 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League semi-finals</a> against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>. Barcelona could only draw 22 against ten men as Chelsea came back from being 02 down; Barcelona eventually lost 23 on aggregate, after already having lost 10 in the first leg at <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 July 2013, the day he celebrated his 25th birthday, Busquets agreed to a new deal until 2018, with the buyout clause remaining unaltered.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 1 August 2014, after the retirement of long time club captain and defender <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puyol" title="Carles Puyol">Carles Puyol</a> and at the veteran's personal request, he was given the number 5 shirt for <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_FC_Barcelona_season" title="201415 FC Barcelona season">the upcoming campaign</a> and was named one of the four captains for the club alongside <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg/170px-2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="184" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg/255px-2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/70/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg/340px-2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg 2x" data-file-width="527" data-file-height="571" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2015_UEFA_Super_Cup_61.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Busquets during the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2015 UEFA Super Cup">2015 UEFA Super Cup</a> against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a></div></div></div>
<p>On 6 June 2015, Busquets started in the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League final</a>, as the team won their fifth accolade in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">the competition</a> by beating <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> 31 at <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_Berlin" class="mw-redirect" title="Olympiastadion Berlin">Olympiastadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> This made Barcelona the first club in history to win <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">the treble</a> of domestic league, domestic cup and European Cup twice, and <a href="/wiki/Dani_Alves" title="Dani Alves">Dani Alves</a>, Busquets, <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pedro_(footballer,_born_July_1987)" class="mw-redirect" title="Pedro (footballer, born July 1987)">Pedro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gerard_Piqu%C3%A9" title="Gerard Piqué">Gerard Piqué</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> the only players to achieve the same feat.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>On 3 October 2015, Busquets captained Barcelona for the first time in the absence of regular captain Iniesta and vice-captain Messi in a 12 <a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_S%C3%A1nchez_Pizju%C3%A1n_Stadium" title="Ramón Sánchez Pizjuán Stadium">away</a> defeat to <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 October 2017, Busquets opened the scoring in a 30 win against <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">Las Palmas</a> which was played inside closed doors at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> due to the ongoing <a href="/wiki/2017_Catalan_independence_referendum" title="2017 Catalan independence referendum">Catalan independence referendum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-theg_Barc_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theg_Barc-40">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Around a year later, he signed a new contract until June 2023, which increased his buyout clause from 200 million to 500 million.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On 24 November 2018 he played his 500th game for Barcelona away to <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> and he made his 100th Champions League appearance on 11 December, in a 11 <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_B" title="201819 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">home</a> draw against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 January 2021, Busquets made his 600th appearance for Barcelona in a 40 win against <a href="/wiki/Granada_CF" title="Granada CF">Granada</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Nuevo_Estadio_de_Los_C%C3%A1rmenes" title="Nuevo Estadio de Los Cármenes">Los Cármenes</a>. Only his contemporaries Xavi, Iniesta and Messi had played more games in the history of the club.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/220px-Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="152" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/330px-Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg/440px-Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="454" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mario_Balotelli_shot_Euro_2012_final_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Busquets playing for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a> in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_final" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Euro 2012 final">Euro 2012 final</a></div></div></div>
<p>On 11 October 2008, Busquets earned his first <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">cap</a> for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-21_football_team" title="Spain national under-21 football team">Spain's under-21</a> in their <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-21_Football_Championship_qualification_play-offs" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-21 Football Championship qualification play-offs">2009 UEFA European Under-21 Football Championship qualification play-offs</a> first-leg away match against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_under-21_football_team" title="Switzerland national under-21 football team">Switzerland</a>. He scored in the 17th minute of a 12 loss,<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> though they eventually emerged victorious 43 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 February 2009, Busquets was called up to the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">senior squad</a> for a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He was named as a substitute for a <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2010 FIFA World Cup qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a> on 28 March 2009,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> making his debut in the return match on 1 April, playing 16 minutes in a 21 win in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> after replacing <a href="/wiki/David_Silva" title="David Silva">David Silva</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:25%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"If I were a player, I would like to be like Busquets."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Vicente del Bosque, June 2010<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Busquets was selected by manager <a href="/wiki/Vicente_del_Bosque" title="Vicente del Bosque">Vicente del Bosque</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>, assuming the holding midfielder role naturalized Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Marcos_Senna" title="Marcos Senna">Marcos Senna</a> had previously occupied in the conquest of <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He played all of the tournament's games and minutes for the eventual world champions, save the last 30 minutes of the 01 group-stage loss against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Durban" title="Durban">Durban</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> He finished the tournament with the thirdhighest pass success rate, alongside his teammate Puyol, completing 88% of his passes.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 8 September 2014, Busquets scored his first international goal in a 51 win over <a href="/wiki/Macedonia_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Macedonia national football team">Macedonia</a> during <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying">Euro 2016's qualifying phase</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> His second came during the same tournament on 15 November, in the 30 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_football_team" title="Belarus national football team">Belarus</a> in <a href="/wiki/Huelva" title="Huelva">Huelva</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 November 2016, Busquets captained Spain for the first time in the absence of regular captain <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos" title="Sergio Ramos">Sergio Ramos</a> in a 22 draw during a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Busquets celebrated his <a href="/wiki/List_of_men%27s_footballers_with_100_or_more_international_caps" title="List of men&#39;s footballers with 100 or more international caps">100th appearance</a> for Spain on 9 October 2017, in a 10 away win against <a href="/wiki/Israel_national_football_team" title="Israel national football team">Israel</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2018 World Cup qualifiers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Subsequently, he was named in <a href="/wiki/Julen_Lopetegui" title="Julen Lopetegui">Julen Lopetegui</a>'s squad for <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">the finals</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:25%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He's one of the greatest talents that has been given to Spanish football. This is a discovery. The first time I saw Busquets playing, I called a friend and said: I saw a player from an extinct species. He's a star."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/C%C3%A9sar_Luis_Menotti" title="César Luis Menotti">César Luis Menotti</a>, July 2011<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Busquets is usually deployed as either a <a href="/wiki/Central_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Central midfielder">central</a> or <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>, although he is also capable of playing as a <a href="/wiki/Central_defender" class="mw-redirect" title="Central defender">central defender</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> A hard-working player, he excels at intercepting loose balls and breaking down opposition plays due to his positional sense, defensive attributes, tackling, tactical intelligence, and ability to read the game, despite his lack of pace.<sup id="cite_ref-Periódico_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Periódico-15">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Supporting_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Supporting-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain&#39;s_Euro_2012_squad_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain&#39;s_Euro_2012_squad-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Due to his vision, ball control, physical prowess, technical skills and accurate passing ability, he rarely relinquishes possession, and alongside both his current and former midfield teammates, such as Iniesta, Xavi and <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Rakiti%C4%87" title="Ivan Rakiti">Ivan Rakiti</a>, he has also played an important creative role in setting his team's tempo in midfield as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deep-lying playmaker</a> through his passing game.<sup id="cite_ref-Supporting_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Supporting-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Changing_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Changing-65">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Manager del Bosque praised Busquets, saying, "If you watch the whole game, you won't see Busquetsbut watch Busquets, and you will see the whole game."<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The latter's height also allows him to be effective in the air, and enables him to advance into more offensive positions on occasion, providing an additional attacking outlet for his team.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
Busquets was largely accused of <a href="/wiki/Diving_(association_football)" title="Diving (association football)">diving</a> by the media on a number of occasions, due to opposition players being wrongly booked or even sent-off during the game because of his excessive play-acting and protests. However, in response to these criticisms, he unabashedly defended diving in football as <i>intelligent</i> play.<sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain&#39;s_Euro_2012_squad_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain&#39;s_Euro_2012_squad-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Often considered to be one of the most underrated footballers in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Busquets earned praise from his peers, with club teammate Messi saying "When there will be trouble, he [Busquets] will be there."<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Busquets' father, <a href="/wiki/Carles_Busquets" title="Carles Busquets">Carles</a>, was also a footballer. He played as a <a href="/wiki/Goalkeeper_(association_football)" title="Goalkeeper (association football)">goalkeeper</a> for Barcelona for several years during the 1990s, although almost exclusively as a backup.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2014, Busquets started a relationship with Elena Galera. In 2016, the couple welcomed their son Enzo.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> He sported an Arabic tattoo on his left forearm translating to "A thing for you, the life in my country", dedicated to his maternal grandfather to whom he was very close.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Sergio_Busquets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Busquets_chilena.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Busquets_chilena.jpg/170px-Busquets_chilena.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="237" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Busquets_chilena.jpg/255px-Busquets_chilena.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Busquets_chilena.jpg/340px-Busquets_chilena.jpg 2x" data-file-width="502" data-file-height="700" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Busquets_chilena.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Busquets executing a <a href="/wiki/Bicycle_kick" title="Bicycle kick">bicycle kick</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a>, 2009</div></div></div>
